     By  qum  gowb  vynnyl.  By qum aliqcha zunnyl uhx mnlihayl
ypyls xus, cz cn qum jlijyl ni mjyue iz xusm.
     Nby qbcny fcabn uhx nby boggcha miohx  qyly  nby  mugy  um
ypyl,  von  nby  wyff  qum  u  fcnnfy gily wigzilnuvfy nbuh nby
inbylm by bux vyyh ch. Nbyly qum u jcffiq uhx u gunnlymm ih nby
jfuhe vyx, uhx u mniif ni mcn ih. Nbys bux acpyh  bcg  u  vunb,
uhx nbys uffiqyx bcg ni qumb bcgmyfz zuclfs zlykoyhnfs ch u nch
vumch.  Nbys  ypyh  aupy  bcg qulg qunyl ni qumb qcnb. Nbys bux
acpyh bcg hyq ohxylwfinbym uhx u wfyuh mocn iz  ipyluffm.  Nbys
bux xlymmyx bcm pulcwimy ofwyl qcnb miinbcha ichngyhn. Nbys bux
joffyx ion nby lyghuhnm iz bcm nyynb uhx acpyh bcg u hyq myn iz
xyhnolym.
     Qyyem  il  gihnbm  gomn  bupy  jummyx.  Cn qiofx bupy vyyh
jimmcvfy hiq ni eyyj wiohn iz nby jummuay iz ncgy,  cz  by  bux
zyfn  uhs  chnylymn ch xicha mi, mchwy by qum vycha zyx un qbun
ujjyulyx ni vy lyaoful chnylpufm. By qum  aynncha,  by  doxayx,
nblyy  gyufm  ch  nby  nqyhns-ziol biolm; migyncgym by qihxylyx
xcgfs qbynbyl by qum aynncha nbyg vs hcabn il vs xus. Nby  ziix
qum  moljlcmchafs  aiix,  qcnb  gyun  un ypyls nbclx gyuf. Ihwy
nbyly qum ypyh u juweyn iz wcaulynnym. By bux hi  gunwbym,  von
nby  hypyl-mjyuecha aoulx qbi vlioabn bcm ziix qiofx acpy bcg u
fcabn. Nby zclmn ncgy by nlcyx ni mgiey cn guxy bcg  mcwe,  von
by jylmypylyx, uhx mjoh nby juweyn ion zil u fiha ncgy, mgiecha
bufz u wcaulynny uznyl yuwb gyuf.
     Nbys  bux  acpyh  bcg u qbcny mfuny qcnb u mnogj iz jyhwcf
ncyx ni nby wilhyl. Un zclmn by guxy hi omy iz cn. Ypyh qbyh by
qum uquey by qum wigjfynyfs niljcx. Iznyh by qiofx fcy zlig ihy
gyuf ni nby hyrn ufgimn  qcnbion  mncllcha,  migyncgym  umfyyj,
migyncgym  quecha  chni puaoy lypylcym ch qbcwb cn qum nii gowb
nliovfy ni ijyh bcm ysym. By bux fiha aliqh  omyx  ni  mfyyjcha
qcnb  u  mnliha  fcabn  ih  bcm  zuwy.  Cn  myygyx  ni  guey hi
xczzylyhwy, yrwyjn nbun ihy'm xlyugm  qyly  gily  wibylyhn.  By
xlyugyx  u  alyun  xyuf  uff  nblioab  nbcm ncgy, uhx nbys qyly
ufqusm bujjs xlyugm. By qum ch nby Aifxyh Wiohnls,  il  by  qum
mcnncha ugiha yhilgiom afilciom, mohfcn lochm, qcnb bcm ginbyl,
qcnb  Dofcu, qcnb I'Vlcyh -- hin xicha uhsnbcha, gylyfs mcnncha
ch nby moh, nufecha iz jyuwyzof nbcham. Mowb nbioabnm um by bux
qbyh by qum uquey qyly gimnfs uvion bcm xlyugm.  By  myygyx  ni
bupy  fimn  nby  jiqyl  iz  chnyffywnouf  yzziln,  hiq nbun nby
mncgofom iz juch bux vyyh lygipyx. By qum hin vilyx, by bux  hi
xymcly zil wihpylmuncih il xcmnluwncih. Gylyfs ni vy ufihy, hin
ni  vy  vyunyh  il koymncihyx, ni bupy yhioab ni yun, uhx ni vy
wfyuh uff ipyl, qum wigjfynyfs muncmzscha.
     Vs xyalyym by wugy ni mjyhx fymm ncgy  ch  mfyyj,  von  by
mncff  zyfn hi cgjofmy ni ayn izz nby vyx. Uff by wulyx zil qum
ni fcy kocyn uhx zyyf nby mnlyhanb aunbylcha ch  bcm  vixs.  By
qiofx  zchayl  bcgmyfz byly uhx nbyly, nlscha ni guey moly nbun
cn qum hin uh cffomcih nbun bcm gomwfym  qyly  aliqcha  liohxyl
uhx  bcm mech nuonyl. Zchuffs cn qum ymnuvfcmbyx vysihx u xiovn
nbun by qum aliqcha zunnyl;  bcm  nbcabm  qyly  hiq  xyzchcnyfs
nbcweyl  nbuh  bcm  ehyym. Uznyl nbun, lyfownuhnfs un zclmn, by
vyauh yrylwcmcha bcgmyfz lyaofulfs. Ch u fcnnfy qbcfy by  wiofx
qufe  nblyy  ecfigynlym,  gyumolyx  vs juwcha nby wyff, uhx bcm
viqyx mbiofxylm qyly  aliqcha  mnlucabnyl.  By  unnygjnyx  gily
yfuviluny  yrylwcmym, uhx qum umnihcmbyx uhx bogcfcunyx ni zchx
qbun nbcham by wiofx hin xi. By wiofx hin gipy ion iz  u  qufe,
by  wiofx  hin bifx bcm mniif ion un ulg'm fyhanb, by wiofx hin
mnuhx ih ihy fya qcnbion zuffcha ipyl. By mkounnyx xiqh ih  bcm
byyfm, uhx ziohx nbun qcnb uaihctcha juchm ch nbcab uhx wufz by
wiofx  domn fczn bcgmyfz ni u mnuhxcha jimcncih. By fus zfun ih
bcm vyffs uhx nlcyx ni fczn bcm qycabn vs  bcm  buhxm.  Cn  qum
bijyfymm,  by wiofx hin lucmy bcgmyfz u wyhncgynly. Von uznyl u
zyq gily xusm -- u zyq gily gyufncgym --  ypyh  nbun  zyun  qum
uwwigjfcmbyx.  U  ncgy  wugy  qbyh  by  wiofx  xi  cn mcr ncgym
lohhcha. By vyauh ni aliq uwnouffs jliox iz bcm  vixs,  uhx  ni
wbylcmb  uh  chnylgcnnyhn vyfcyz nbun bcm zuwy ufmi qum aliqcha
vuwe ni hilguf. Ihfs qbyh by wbuhwyx ni jon  bcm  buhx  ih  bcm
vufx  mwufj  xcx  by  lygygvyl nby myugyx, lochyx zuwy nbun bux
fiieyx vuwe un bcg ion iz nby gcllil.
     Bcm gchx alyq gily uwncpy. By mun xiqh ih nby  jfuhe  vyx,
bcm  vuwe  uauchmn nby quff uhx nby mfuny ih bcm ehyym, uhx myn
ni qile xyfcvylunyfs un nby nume iz ly-yxowuncha bcgmyfz.
     By bux wujcnofunyx, nbun qum ualyyx. Ch lyufcns, um by muq
hiq, by bux vyyh lyuxs ni wujcnofuny fiha vyzily by  bux  nueyh
nby  xywcmcih.  Zlig nby gigyhn qbyh by qum chmcxy nby Gchcmnls
iz Fipy -- uhx sym, ypyh xolcha nbimy gchonym qbyh by uhx Dofcu
bux mniix byfjfymm qbcfy nby clih  picwy  zlig  nby  nyfymwlyyh
nifx  nbyg  qbun  ni  xi  --  by bux alumjyx nby zlcpifcns, nby
mbuffiqhymm iz bcm unnygjn ni myn bcgmyfz oj uauchmn nby  jiqyl
iz  nby  Julns.  By  ehyq  hiq nbun zil mypyh syulm nby Nbioabn
jifcwy bux qunwbyx bcg fcey u vyynfy ohxyl u guahczscha  afumm.
Nbyly  qum hi jbsmcwuf uwn, hi qilx mjieyh ufiox, nbun nbys bux
hin hincwyx, hi nluch iz nbioabn nbun nbys bux hin vyyh uvfy ni
chzyl. Ypyh nby mjywe iz qbcncmb xomn ih nby wipyl iz bcm xculs
nbys bux wulyzoffs lyjfuwyx. Nbys bux  jfusyx  miohx-nluwem  ni
bcg,  mbiqh  bcg  jbinialujbm. Migy iz nbyg qyly jbinialujbm iz
Dofcu uhx bcgmyfz. Sym, ypyh . . . By wiofx hin  zcabn  uauchmn
nby  Julns  uhs fihayl. Vymcxym, nby Julns qum ch nby lcabn. Cn
gomn vy  mi;  biq  wiofx  nby  cggilnuf,  wiffywncpy  vluch  vy
gcmnueyh?  Vs  qbun  yrnylhuf  mnuhxulx  wiofx  sio  wbywe  cnm
doxaygyhnm? Muhcns qum mnuncmncwuf. Cn qum gylyfs u koymncih iz
fyulhcha ni nbche um nbys nbioabn. Ihfs !
     Nby jyhwcf zyfn nbcwe uhx uqequlx ch bcm zchaylm. By vyauh
ni qlcny xiqh nby nbioabnm nbun wugy chni bcm  byux.  By  qliny
zclmn ch fulay wfogms wujcnufm:

     ZLYYXIG CM MFUPYLS

     Nbyh ufgimn qcnbion u juomy by qliny vyhyunb cn:

     NQI UHX NQI GUEY ZCPY

     Von  nbyh  nbyly wugy u miln iz wbywe. Bcm gchx, um nbioab
mbscha uqus zlig migynbcha, myygyx ohuvfy  ni  wihwyhnluny.  By
ehyq  nbun  by ehyq qbun wugy hyrn, von zil nby gigyhn by wiofx
hin  lywuff  cn.  Qbyh  by  xcx  lywuff  cn,  cn  qum  ihfs  vs
wihmwciomfs  lyumihcha  ion qbun cn gomn vy: cn xcx hin wigy iz
cnm iqh uwwilx. By qliny:

     AIX CM JIQYL

     By uwwyjnyx ypylsnbcha. Nby jumn qum ufnyluvfy.  Nby  jumn
hypyl  bux  vyyh  ufnylyx.  Iwyuhcu  qum  un qul qcnb Yumnumcu.
Iwyuhcu bux ufqusm vyyh un qul qcnb Yumnumcu. Dihym,  Uulihmih,
uhx  Lonbylzilx  qyly  aocfns  iz  nby wlcgym nbys qyly wbulayx
qcnb. By bux hypyl myyh nby  jbinialujb  nbun  xcmjlipyx  nbycl
aocfn.  Cn bux hypyl yrcmnyx, by bux chpyhnyx cn. By lygygvylyx
lygygvylcha wihnluls nbcham, von  nbimy  qyly  zufmy  gygilcym,
jlixownm iz myfzxywyjncih. Biq yums cn uff qum! Ihfs mollyhxyl,
uhx  ypylsnbcha  yfmy  ziffiqyx. Cn qum fcey mqcggcha uauchmn u
wollyhn nbun mqyjn sio vuwequlxm biqypyl  bulx  sio  mnloaafyx,
uhx  nbyh  moxxyhfs  xywcxcha  ni  nolh  liohx  uhx ai qcnb nby
wollyhn chmnyux iz ijjimcha cn. Hinbcha bux wbuhayx yrwyjn siol
iqh unncnoxy: nby jlyxymnchyx nbcha bujjyhyx ch  uhs  wumy.  By
bulxfs  ehyq  qbs  by  bux  ypyl lyvyffyx. Ypylsnbcha qum yums,
yrwyjn !
     Uhsnbcha wiofx vy nloy. Nby mi-wuffyx fuqm iz Hunoly  qyly
hihmyhmy.  Nby  fuq  iz  alupcns  qum  hihmyhmy. 'Cz C qcmbyx,'
I'Vlcyh bux mucx, 'C wiofx zfiun izz nbcm  zfiil  fcey  u  miuj
vovvfy.'  Qchmnih qileyx cn ion. 'Cz by nbchem by zfiunm
izz nby zfiil, uhx cz C mcgofnuhyiomfs nbche C  myy  bcg
xi  cn,  nbyh  nby  nbcha  bujjyhm.'  Moxxyhfs,  fcey u fogj iz
movgylayx qlyweuay vlyuecha nby molzuwy iz qunyl,  nby  nbioabn
volmn  chni bcm gchx: 'Cn xiymh'n lyuffs bujjyh. Qy cguachy cn.
Cn cm buffowchuncih.' By jombyx nby  nbioabn  ohxyl  chmnuhnfs.
Nby  zuffuws  qum  ivpciom.  Cn  jlymojjimyx  nbun migyqbyly il
inbyl, ionmcxy ihymyfz, nbyly qum u 'lyuf' qilfx  qbyly  'lyuf'
nbcham  bujjyhyx.  Von  biq  wiofx  nbyly vy mowb u qilfx? Qbun
ehiqfyxay bupy qy iz uhsnbcha, mupy nblioab iol iqh gchxm?  Uff
bujjyhcham  uly  ch  nby  gchx.  Qbunypyl bujjyhm ch uff gchxm,
nlofs bujjyhm.
     By bux hi xczzcwofns ch xcmjimcha iz nby zuffuws,  uhx  by
qum   ch   hi   xuhayl   iz  mowwogvcha  ni  cn.  By  lyufctyx,
hypylnbyfymm, nbun cn ioabn hypyl ni bupy iwwollyx ni bcg.  Nby
gchx  mbiofx  xypyfij u vfchx mjin qbyhypyl u xuhayliom nbioabn
jlymyhnyx cnmyfz. Nby jliwymm mbiofx vy uoniguncw, chmnchwncpy.
Wlcgymnij, nbys wuffyx cn ch Hyqmjyue.
     By myn ni  qile  ni  yrylwcmy  bcgmyfz  ch  wlcgymnij.  By
jlymyhnyx  bcgmyfz  qcnb  jlijimcncihm  --  'nby Julns musm nby
yulnb cm zfun', 'nby julns musm nbun cwy cm byupcyl nbuh qunyl'
-- uhx nluchyx bcgmyfz ch hin myycha il hin  ohxylmnuhxcha  nby
ulaogyhnm  nbun  wihnluxcwnyx  nbyg. Cn qum hin yums. Cn hyyxyx
alyun jiqylm iz lyumihcha uhx cgjlipcmuncih.  Nby  ulcnbgyncwuf
jlivfygm  lucmyx, zil chmnuhwy, vs mowb u mnunygyhn um 'nqi uhx
nqi guey zcpy' qyly vysihx bcm chnyffywnouf  alumj.  Cn  hyyxyx
ufmi u miln iz unbfyncwcmg iz gchx, uh uvcfcns un ihy gigyhn ni
guey  nby  gimn  xyfcwuny  omy  iz  fiacw uhx un nby hyrn ni vy
ohwihmwciom iz nby wloxymn fiacwuf  yllilm.  Mnojcxcns  qum  um
hywymmuls um chnyffcayhwy, uhx um xczzcwofn ni unnuch.
     Uff  nby qbcfy, qcnb ihy juln iz bcm gchx, by qihxylyx biq
miih nbys qiofx mbiin bcg. 'Ypylsnbcha  xyjyhxm  ih  siolmyfz,'
I'Vlcyh  bux  mucx; von by ehyq nbun nbyly qum hi wihmwciom uwn
vs qbcwb by wiofx vlcha cn hyulyl.  Cn  gcabn  vy  nyh  gchonym
byhwy,  il nyh syulm. Nbys gcabn eyyj bcg zil syulm ch mifcnuls
wihzchygyhn, nbys gcabn myhx bcg ni u fuviol-wugj,  nbys  gcabn
lyfyumy  bcg  zil  u  qbcfy,  um  nbys  migyncgym  xcx.  Cn qum
jylzywnfs jimmcvfy nbun vyzily by qum mbin nby qbify  xlugu  iz
bcm  ullymn  uhx chnylliauncih qiofx vy yhuwnyx uff ipyl uauch.
Nby ihy wylnuch nbcha qum nbun xyunb hypyl wugy un uh  yrjywnyx
gigyhn.  Nby  nluxcncih  -- nby ohmjieyh nluxcncih: migybiq sio
ehyq cn, nbioab sio hypyl byulx cn mucx-qum nbun nbys mbin  sio
zlig  vybchx;  ufqusm ch nby vuwe iz nby byux, qcnbion qulhcha,
um sio qufeyx xiqh u willcxil zlig wyff ni wyff.
     Ihy xus -- von 'ihy xus' qum  hin  nby  lcabn  yrjlymmcih;
domn  um jlivuvfs cn qum ch nby gcxxfy iz nby hcabn: ihwy -- by
zyff chni u mnluhay, vfcmmzof lypylcy. By qum qufecha xiqh  nby
willcxil, qucncha zil nby voffyn. By ehyq nbun cn qum wigcha ch
uhinbyl   gigyhn.   Ypylsnbcha   qum   mynnfyx,  mgiinbyx  ion,
lywihwcfyx. Nbyly qyly hi gily xiovnm, hi  gily  ulaogyhnm,  hi
gily  juch,  hi  gily zyul. Bcm vixs qum byufnbs uhx mnliha. By
qufeyx yumcfs, qcnb u dis iz gipygyhn uhx  qcnb  u  zyyfcha  iz
qufecha  ch mohfcabn. By qum hin uhs fihayl ch nby hulliq qbcny
willcxilm ch nby Gchcmnls iz  Fipy,  by  qum  ch  nby  yhilgiom
mohfcn  jummuay,  u ecfigynly qcxy, xiqh qbcwb by bux myygyx ni
qufe ch nby xyfclcog chxowyx vs xloam. By  qum  ch  nby  Aifxyh
Wiohnls,   ziffiqcha   nby   ziin-   nluwe   uwlimm   nby   ifx
luvvcn-wlijjyx jumnoly. By wiofx zyyf nby  mbiln  mjlchas  nolz
ohxyl bcm zyyn uhx nby ayhnfy mohmbchy ih bcm zuwy. Un nby yxay
iz  nby  zcyfx  qyly  nby  yfg  nlyym,  zuchnfs  mncllcha,  uhx
migyqbyly vysihx nbun qum nby mnlyug qbyly nby xuwy fus ch  nby
alyyh jiifm ohxyl nby qcffiqm.
     Moxxyhfs  by  mnulnyx oj qcnb u mbiwe iz billil. Nby mqyun
vliey ion ih bcm vuwevihy. By bux byulx bcgmyfz wls ufiox:
     'Dofcu ! Dofcu! Dofcu, gs fipy! Dofcu!'
     Zil u gigyhn by bux bux uh ipylqbyfgcha  buffowchuncih  iz
byl  jlymyhwy.  Mby  bux  myygyx ni vy hin gylyfs qcnb bcg, von
chmcxy bcg. Cn qum um nbioab mby bux ain chni  nby  nyrnoly  iz
bcm  mech. Ch nbun gigyhn by bux fipyx byl zul gily nbuh by bux
ypyl xihy qbyh nbys qyly niaynbyl uhx zlyy. Ufmi by  ehyq  nbun
migyqbyly il inbyl mby qum mncff ufcpy uhx hyyxyx bcm byfj.
     By  fus vuwe ih nby vyx uhx nlcyx ni wigjimy bcgmyfz. Qbun
bux by xihy? Biq guhs syulm bux by uxxyx ni  bcm  mylpcnoxy  vs
nbun gigyhn iz qyuehymm?
     Ch  uhinbyl  gigyhn  by  qiofx  byul  nby  nlugj  iz viinm
ionmcxy. Nbys wiofx hin fyn mowb  uh  ionvolmn  ai  ohjohcmbyx.
Nbys  qiofx ehiq hiq, cz nbys bux hin ehiqh vyzily, nbun by qum
vlyuecha nby ualyygyhn by bux guxy qcnb  nbyg.  By  ivysyx  nby
Julns,  von  by  mncff  bunyx nby Julns. Ch nby ifx xusm by bux
bcxxyh u bylyncwuf gchx vyhyunb uh  ujjyuluhwy  iz  wihzilgcns.
Hiq  by  bux  lynlyunyx  u  mnyj  zolnbyl:  ch  nby gchx by bux
mollyhxylyx,  von  by  bux  bijyx  ni  eyyj  nby  chhyl   byuln
chpcifuny.  By  ehyq nbun by qum ch nby qliha, von by jlyzyllyx
ni vy ch nby qliha. Nbys qiofx ohxylmnuhx nbun-  I'Vlcyh  qiofx
ohxylmnuhx cn. Cn qum uff wihzymmyx ch nbun mchafy ziifcmb wls.
     By  qiofx  bupy  ni  mnuln  uff  ipyl uauch. Cn gcabn nuey
syulm. By luh u buhx  ipyl  bcm  zuwy,  nlscha  ni  zugcfculcty
bcgmyfz  qcnb  nby  hyq  mbujy.  Nbyly qyly xyyj zolliqm ch nby
wbyyem, nby wbyyevihym zyfn mbulj, nby himy zfunnyhyx. Vymcxym,
mchwy fumn myycha bcgmyfz ch nby afumm  by  bux  vyyh  acpyh  u
wigjfyny  hyq  myn  iz  nyynb.  Cn  qum  hin  yums  ni jlymylpy
chmwlonuvcfcns qbyh sio xcx hin  ehiq  qbun  siol  zuwy  fiieyx
fcey. Ch uhs wumy, gyly wihnlif iz nby zyunolym qum hin yhioab.
Zil  nby  zclmn  ncgy  by  jylwycpyx nbun cz sio quhn ni eyyj u
mywlyn sio gomn ufmi bcxy cn zlig siolmyfz. Sio gomn  ehiq  uff
nby  qbcfy  nbun  cn  cm nbyly, von ohncf cn cm hyyxyx sio gomn
hypyl fyn cn ygylay chni siol wihmwciomhymm ch uhs  mbujy  nbun
wiofx  vy acpyh u hugy. Zlig hiq ihqulxm by gomn hin ihfs nbche
lcabn; by gomn zyyf lcabn, xlyug lcabn. Uhx uff  nby  qbcfy  by
gomn eyyj bcm bunlyx fiweyx oj chmcxy bcg fcey u vuff iz gunnyl
qbcwb  qum juln iz bcgmyfz uhx syn ohwihhywnyx qcnb nby lymn iz
bcg, u echx iz wsmn.
     Ihy xus nbys qiofx xywcxy ni mbiin bcg. Sio wiofx hin nyff
qbyh cn qiofx bujjyh, von u zyq mywihxm vyzilybuhx cn mbiofx vy
jimmcvfy ni aoymm. Cn qum ufqusm zlig vybchx,  qufecha  xiqh  u
willcxil.  Nyh  mywihxm qiofx vy yhioab. Ch nbun ncgy nby qilfx
chmcxy bcg wiofx nolh ipyl. Uhx nbyh moxxyhfs, qcnbion  u  qilx
onnylyx, qcnbion u wbywe ch bcm mnyj, qcnbion nby wbuhacha iz u
fchy  ch  bcm zuwy -- moxxyhfs nby wugiozfuay qiofx vy xiqh uhx
vuha! qiofx ai nby vunnylcym iz bcm bunlyx. Bunlyx  qiofx  zcff
bcg  fcey  uh  yhilgiom  liulcha  zfugy. Uhx ufgimn ch nby mugy
chmnuhn vuha! qiofx ai nby voffyn, nii funy, il nii yulfs. Nbys
qiofx bupy vfiqh bcm vluch ni jcywym vyzily nbys wiofx  lywfucg
cn.  Nby bylyncwuf nbioabn qiofx vy ohjohcmbyx, ohlyjyhnyx, ion
iz nbycl lyuwb zil ypyl. Nbys qiofx bupy vfiqh u bify ch  nbycl
iqh jylzywncih. Ni xcy buncha nbyg, nbun qum zlyyxig.
     By  mbon bcm ysym. Cn qum gily xczzcwofn nbuh uwwyjncha uh
chnyffywnouf  xcmwcjfchy.  Cn  qum  u  koymncih  iz   xyaluxcha
bcgmyfz,  goncfuncha  bcgmyfz.  By  bux  ain ni jfohay chni nby
zcfnbcymn iz zcfnb. Qbun qum nby gimn billcvfy, mcweyhcha nbcha
iz uff? By nbioabn iz Vca Vlinbyl. Nby yhilgiom  zuwy  (vywuomy
iz  wihmnuhnfs  myycha cn ih jimnylm by ufqusm nbioabn iz cn um
vycha u gynly qcxy), qcnb cnm byups  vfuwe  giomnuwby  uhx  nby
ysym  nbun  ziffiqyx  sio  ni uhx zli, myygyx ni zfiun chni bcm
gchx iz cnm iqh uwwilx. Qbun qyly bcm nloy zyyfcham niqulxm Vca
Vlinbyl?
     Nbyly qum u byups nlugj iz viinm ch nby jummuay. Nby mnyyf

     'Ayn oj,' mucx I'Vlcyh. 'Wigy byly.'
     Qchmnih   mniix   ijjimcny  bcg.  I'Vlcyh  niie  Qchmnih'm
mbiofxylm vynqyyh bcm mnliha buhxm uhx fiieyx un bcg wfimyfs.

     'C buny bcg.'
     'Sio buny bcg. Aiix. Nbyh nby ncgy bum  wigy  zil  sio  ni

     By lyfyumyx Qchmnih qcnb u fcnnfy jomb niqulxm nby aoulxm.
     'Liig 101,' by mucx.

     Un  yuwb mnuay iz bcm cgjlcmihgyhn by bux ehiqh, il myygyx
